# GPU — hexa-lang's NVPTX-first GPU substrate (domain SSOT)

> One-file roadmap + cycle ledger for the GPU codegen substrate
> (RFC 055 + RFC 067/068/069 chain + ongoing follow-ons). Domain
> SSOT per `AGENTS.tape` `@D g_plan_consolidation`: cycle-by-cycle
> progression appended to `compiler/PLAN.md`; this file is the
> *forward-looking checklist* + *brainstorm-to-exhaustion roadmap*.

**hexa-lang North-Star ① (NN stack)** + **§12 P4+ chain** + **GOAL — "cuBLAS-using stacks 를 whole-program-fusion 으로 우회"** are the umbrella metrics this file tracks.

---

## 0 · One-paragraph state (end-of-day 2026-05-20)

§12 P4+ chain end-to-end functional: codegen-side (hexa MIR → PTX) and silicon-side (PTX → ptxas → RTX 5070 sm_120 driver-JIT → numeric correctness) both **measured-PASS**. 25 PRs landed today including the **first three ever §12 P4+ silicon-fire closures** (RFC 067 WMMA, RFC 068 f16, RFC 069 unroll byte-eq) + codegen↔silicon reconcile (PR #193). `nvptx_lower_test` smoke: 9/9 → 25/25 cases this session.

---

## 1 · Completed (measured-PASS, landed on origin/main)

### 1a — codegen scaffolding (RFC 055 §1-§12 P3)

- [x] **RFC 055 Stage-1 scaffold** — NVPTX target enum, PTX opcode table, address-space constants, target enum dispatch
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P0** — PTX text emit pass for FP64-arithmetic subset (`add.f64`, `mul.f64`, `mov.f64`, `ret`, `.func`, `.reg .f64`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P1** — `@gpu_kernel` end-to-end vec-add slice (`.visible .entry`, `.param .u64`, `ld.global.f64`, `st.global.f64`, `mov.u32 %tid.x`, address arithmetic, bounds-check `setp + bra`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P2** — naive FP64 GEMM `@gpu_kernel` (i-j-k loop, FMA-ready)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3a** — `--target=nvptx64-nvidia-cuda-sm{80,90}` dispatch in `compiler/main.hexa`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3b** — per-Local PTX register-kind classification (`.f64` / `.u32` / `.u64` / `.pred`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3b** — `STMT_BR` / `STMT_BR_COND` / `STMT_CALL gpu_*` / `STMT_LOAD` / `STMT_STORE` generic lowering
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3c** — `@gpu_kernel` / `@gpu_device` partition (`gpu_kind` field on `MFunc`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4** — `gpu_barrier()` block-wide sync (`bar.sync 0;`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** — `gpu_atomic_add()` global `atom.add.f64`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** — `gpu_warp_shuffle()` `shfl.sync.idx.b32`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** — Tensor Core MMA scaffold (NVPTX_RKIND_FRAG, `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` table, STMT_CALL recognition)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** — mixed-precision scaffold (NVPTX_RKIND_F16/_BF16/_F32, classifier rules)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** — `_nvptx_unroll_pass` MVP (canonical 3-block back-edge, factor=2)

### 1b — RFC 067 (real WMMA emit)

- [x] **P0** — Shape-B RFC draft + marker comments (PR #138)
- [x] **P1** — Fragment-as-tile-vector (8 `.reg .b32 %fra<id>_e<i>`) + `F-RFC067-FRAG-WIDTH` PASS (PR #150)
- [x] **P2** — `.shared .align 16 .b8 _hexa_wmma_stage_<fn>[2048]` decl + `F-RFC067-SHARED-DECL` PASS (PR #155)
- [x] **P3** — PReg fragment role + dtype + layout metadata + `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic_family` re-key + `F-RFC067-DTYPE-FAMILY` PASS (PR #170)
- [x] **INSTR-EMIT** — Real `wmma.load.a/b`, `wmma.mma`, `wmma.store.d` PTX (replaces scaffold-comment stub) (PR #177)
- [x] **P4 silicon** — single-tile 16x16 GEMM Tensor Core fire vs FP32 ref, `max|Δ|=0`, `F-RFC067-TILE-LOOP-NUMERIC` PASS (PR #191)

### 1c — RFC 068 (mixed-precision MIR layer)

- [x] **P0** — Shape-B RFC draft + marker comments (PR #140)
- [x] **P1** — Local.precision tag thread + classifier short-circuit + `F-RFC068-PRECISION-PROPAGATE` PASS (PR #148)
- [x] **P2** — HIR `@f16`/`@bf16`/`@f32` named-type primitives + `_op_with_precision` opcode-suffix generation + `F-RFC068-OPCODE-SUFFIX` PASS (PR #170)
- [x] **P3** — body-emit `add.f16/.bf16/.f32` mnemonics + `F-RFC068-BODY-MNEMONIC` PASS (PR #175)
- [x] **P4-prereq** — `ld.global.<ty>` / `st.global.<ty>` codegen seam + `F-RFC068-LD-ST-CODEGEN` PASS (PR #186)
- [x] **P4 silicon** — f16 vec-add silicon fire vs FP16-roundtrip ref, `max|Δ|=0/1024`, `F-RFC068-NUMERIC-EQ` PASS (PR #189)
- [x] **codegen↔silicon reconcile** — ptxas accepts `.b16` storage but rejects `ld.global.f16`; constants reconciled (PR #193)

### 1d — RFC 069 (advanced loop unroll)

- [x] **P0** — Shape-B RFC draft + marker comments (PR #141)
- [x] **P1** — factor=N parameterization (2 ≤ N ≤ 32) + `F-RFC069-FACTOR-N` PASS (PR #147)
- [x] **P2** — multi-exit loop matcher (STMT_BR_COND back-edge in either arm) + `F-RFC069-MULTI-EXIT-MATCH` PASS (PR #156)
- [x] **P3** — nested-loop detection + honest passthrough preservation + `F-RFC069-NESTED-PRESERVE` PASS (PR #159)
- [x] **wiring** — `HEXA_NVPTX_UNROLL_FACTOR` env-gated codegen pipeline integration + GEMM K-loop MIR fixture (PR #179)
- [x] **P4 silicon** — unroll=1 vs unroll=2 vec-add byte-eq on RTX 5070, `byte_mismatch=0/1024`, `F-RFC069-NUMERIC-EQ` PASS (PR #190)

### 1i — Codegen correctness coverage (2026-05-26) 🛸

Source-to-silicon **arithmetic/operator coverage** closure — the silent-miscompile
class where the frontend produces an op the NVPTX codegen never wired (dst register
left unset → garbage), or wired with a ptxas-illegal mnemonic. All verified via
`nvptx_lower_test` compiled-path (mac arm64) + archive ptxas-ground-truth / ubu-2 fire.

- [x] **wmma scaffold mnemonic grammar** (PR #1189) — `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` + `_family` emitted ptxas-illegal forms (`.f16.shared` state-space-after-type · long `.f32.f16.f16.f32` for f16 multiplicand). Fixed to `.shared.f16` + short `.f32.f32`/`.f16.f16`; bf16 long form kept. Test asserts had lock-in'd the buggy strings (N122 b1+b2).
- [x] **integer `/` `%`** (PR #1193, RE-LANDED after `9652fd5e` silent-wipe) — `div.s32`/`div.s64` + `rem.s32`/`rem.s64` in `_nvptx_binop_mnemonic_for_kind`; was falling through to FP64 `div.rn.f64` (ptxas-illegal on int regs → N70 GAP-B hang).
- [x] **integer bitwise/shift** (PR #1207) — `& | ^ << >>` → `and/or/xor.b{32,64}` · `shl.b{32,64}` · `shr.s{32,64}`. Enables masking/packing/quantization/Hilbert-d2xy bit-math @gpu_kernels.
- [x] **FP32 division** (PR #1210) — `div_f32` → `div.rn.f32` (the documented "future codegen-side div row"). ML kernels (softmax `e/Σe`, layernorm `x/√var`). f16/bf16 div = honest stub (no native PTX mnemonic).
- [x] **sm_120 `.version` 8.0 → 8.7** (PR #1202) — bare sm_120 declared an ISA version the RTX 5070 driver-JIT rejects for matmul/WMMA (N153-fire finding); unified with the sm_120a (TMA) 8.7 pin.
- [x] **GPU math intrinsics** (PR #1215) 🛸 — `sqrt`/`rsqrt`/`max`/`min`/`abs`/`exp` STMT_CALLs were hitting `// unsupported call` stub (latent incomplete ML kernels). Now wired: EXACT `sqrt.rn.{f32,f64}` · `max`/`min.{f32,f64,s32,s64}` · `abs.{f32,f64}`; APPROX `rsqrt.approx.f32` + `exp` = `mul.f32 ·log2e` → `ex2.approx.f32`; f64 rsqrt/exp = honest stub (no native PTX). Classifier Pass-1 inherits operand bank ([f32]→.f32 family). **ubu-2 RTX 5070 silicon**: sqrt/max/min/abs byte-eq 0/1024; rsqrt/exp max_rel ≤ 1.74e-7 / 4.76e-7 (within PTX 9.7.3 `.approx` 2^-21 HW bound). nvptx_lower_test 38/38.

> **✅ Codegen correctness/coverage lane COMPLETE** — every operator/intrinsic the frontend can produce inside a `@gpu_kernel` is now wired or honest-stubbed (int +−×÷%·bitwise·shift · FP +−×÷ · math sqrt/rsqrt/max/min/abs/exp · wmma · shuffle idx/xor/FP64 · atomic_add · thread-ids · matmul explicit+natural-loop). Further `gpu_*` builtins (shuffle down/up, atomic max/min/cas) have NO frontend consumer → speculative, not actionable without prior builtin registration.

**Remaining domain frontier (terminal / out-of-foreground-scope):** §10 production-driver E2E (`hexa build src --target=nvptx`) blocked by Mac self-host OOM (`project_compiler_selfbuild_blockers`) — codegen emit + silicon already proven (N128/N153/N71-B); SGEMM perf at documented local-optimum (64×64+Hilbert, every larger-tile/wgmma/split-K/warp-spec lever falsified); ROCm multi-vendor HW-blocked ($0 AMD inventory); whole-program-fusion sub-threshold launch-bound win (R12, live research lane).

- [x] **F-RFC069-PASSTHROUGH-PRESERVED** — Case 11 (non-matching CFG passthrough) byte-identical across the RFC 069 P1-P3 cycle

### 1f — Crash-recovery cycle (2026-05-21)

Recovery cycle after macOS crash lost two in-flight stash diffs (rounds 5-8 GPU.md doc + RFC 071 P2.1 spec, both unpushed). The original artifact directories referenced from those stashes (`rfc067_p9_rounds_5_7_2026_05_21/`, `rfc067_pA_round8_2026_05_21/`, `rfc067_p6_revalidate_2026_05_21/`) were lost system-wide. Stash patches preserved at `docs/notes/crash_recovery_2026_05_21/`. Re-fired the idempotent subset on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120; new artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pB_crash_recovered_2026_05_21/`.

- [x] **F-RFC067-PB-ORACLE-BATTERY** — 8/9 hand-emit PTX smokes ptxas_rc=0 on ubu-2 (sm_80 + sm_90 mixed): `vprintf` · `__assertfail` · `atom.shared.add.s32` · `ldmatrix.sync.aligned.x4.m8n8.shared.b16` · `mbarrier.init.shared::cta.b64` (sm_90) · `wmma.mma.sync...m16n16k16.f16.f16` · `wmma.mma.sync...m16n16k16.f32.bf16.bf16.f32` · `bar.sync 0` (coop_launch). 1 honest fail: `cp.async.bulk.shared::cta.global` → "State space incorrect" (TMA needs full tensor descriptor + mbarrier rendezvous, not the bulk-copy primitive in isolation). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pB_crash_recovered_2026_05_21/oracle_ptx/oracle_results.txt`
- [x] **F-RFC067-PB-COOKBOOK-REVALIDATE** — 6/6 cookbook PTX ptxas_rc=0 with per-file `.target` arch auto-detect (sm_80 + sm_90). SASS instr counts (measured by `cuobjdump --dump-sass` line-count): step1_single_tile=80 (sm_80) · step2_multitile=320 (sm_90) · step3_multiwarp=336 (sm_90) · step4_cp_async=256 (sm_90) · step5_tf32=144 (sm_80) · composite_perf=352 (sm_90). PR #214 composite kernel (`wmma_256x256_grid.ptx`) re-validates cleanly. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pB_crash_recovered_2026_05_21/cookbook_revalidate/result.txt`

Telemetry: 38 °C · 6.28 W · 210/210/405 MHz (gr/sm/mem) idle. Toolkit: nvcc 12.0.140 · ptxas V12.0.140 · driver 580.126.09

- [x] **HGEMM scale-up matrix M=N=K=256/384/512/768/1024 cuBLAS baseline + hexa M=256 re-fire** — 200 timed launches per shape on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (cudaEventRecord per-launch sync, 20 warmup). cuBLAS GemmEx HGEMM TFLOPS: **256→4.59 · 384→13.11 · 512→25.04 · 768→46.45 · 1024→52.25**. Hexa-emit not firable at M≥384 (shape-locked; needs new codegen invocation per shape, multi-session). cuBLAS scales linearly with M while hexa-emit's single-shape coverage caps the ratio claim; honest scope = "MET at M=256 · scale-up tested on cuBLAS side · hexa-side gap requires variable-shape kernel emission". Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pC_hgemm_scaleup_2026_05_21/`. Honest stash correction (`@D g3`): pre-crash stash 0 numbers (4.08/11.05/10.92/17.02/15.66 hexa · 8.17/18.4/32.7/55.2/55.8 cuBLAS · ratios 0.50/0.60/0.33/0.31/0.28) RETRACTED — both sides slower today; ratio reversed direction at M=256 (0.77 today vs 0.50 stash); only the **shape of cuBLAS scaling curve** broadly agrees with stash trend
- [x] **F-RFC071-MIR-DRIVER-INVOKE** — RFC 071 P2.1 wiring landed (`compiler/cli/build_nvptx.hexa` cherry-pick from worktree `321f893a`). `_build_nvptx_stub_ptx` body flipped from canned text to `codegen_emit_ptx_sm80(_build_hand_mir_vec_add())` — first real codegen invocation from the emit-driver. `_build_hand_mir_vec_add()` synthesises the 055-P3c MFunc shape (`gpu_kind = GPU_KIND_KERNEL` · 4 params a/b/c/n · STMT_LOAD ×2 · STMT_BINOP "add" · STMT_STORE · STMT_RETURN) mirroring `compiler/codegen/nvptx_emit_test.hexa`'s known-good builder. Substring assertions traced statically through `_emit_ptx_func` (L1583/1588) + `_nvptx_lower_stmt` STMT_LOAD/STORE (L714/729) + `_nvptx_ld_mnem_for_kind`/`_nvptx_st_mnem_for_kind` (L329/342): `.visible .entry` + `.param .u64` ×4 + `ld.global.f64` + `add.f64` + `st.global.f64` ALL produced by construction. `hexa parse compiler/cli/build_nvptx.hexa` rc=0. `F-RFC055-CPU-CODEGEN-UNTOUCHED` preserved (CPU codegen files MD5-identical pre/post). Honest scope: emitted PTX reflects hardcoded vec-add MIR, NOT `src_path` source bytes (P3 module-loader bridge is the next stop). `sm_arch` parameter accepted but not threaded — sm_80 hardcoded; sm_90/sm_120 dispatch flip = follow-on
- **F-RFC071-E2E-NUMERIC-EQ (P4 silicon)** — still deferred (multi-session). The P2.1 chain proves `cmd_build --target=nvptx64-*` → `_build_nvptx_emit_driver` → real PTX text emission, but the PTX content is a hardcoded vec-add MIR fixture not derived from the input `.hexa` source file. Full source-to-silicon e2e closure requires P3 module-loader bridge (`@gpu_kernel` annotation parsing + MFunc partitioning) + P4 ubu-2 silicon fire of the auto-emitted PTX. §10 closure box stays `[ ]` until P4 PASSes
- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SHAPES-NUMERIC-EQ** 🛸 — Metal codegen extended from 1 → 3 recognised shapes (`compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa` cherry-pick from worktree `92b2dcbb`: vec-add (original) + vec-mul `c[i] = a[i]*b[i]` + vec-scale `c[i] = a[i]*const`). 6/6 `metal_lower_test.hexa` cases PASS (sub-agent build+run on isolated worktree). Local 3-shape silicon-fire on Apple M3 (hand-emit .metal matching each codegen shape) PASSES ALL: vec_add max|Δ|=0 byte_mm=0/1024 · vec_mul max|Δ|=0 byte_mm=0/1024 · vec_scale max|Δ|=0 byte_mm=0/1024. Single Swift host loads 3 metallibs sequentially. New falsifiers `F-RFC075-METAL-EMIT-VEC-MUL` + `F-RFC075-METAL-EMIT-VEC-SCALE` (15-substring batteries + negative `_check_not_contains(" + ")` guards). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_p4_shapes_2026_05_21/`
- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SHAPES-SCALEUP-NUMERIC-EQ** 🛸 — 3-shape × 7-size scale-up on Apple M3: vec_add / vec_mul / vec_scale × N∈{1K, 4K, 16K, 64K, 256K, 1M, 4M}. 5 warmup + 50 timed dispatches per (shape, N). **21/21 byte_eq with CPU reference**. Peak effective bandwidth at N=4M: vec_mul **39.94 GB/s** · vec_add **34.59 GB/s** · vec_scale **22.34 GB/s** (lower because `vec_scale.metal` is hardcoded with 3-buffer dispatch ABI but only reads buf-a + writes buf-c — formula `3·N·4/median` overcounts; corrected 2·N·4 would put vec_scale around 14.89 GB/s, consistent with bytes-moved). Re-measured vec_add 4M = 34.59 GB/s vs earlier (commit `9ee6d020`) 50.53 GB/s — system state drift (thermal / scheduling), both honest. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_shapes_scaleup_2026_05_21/`
- [x] **F-RFC067-COOKBOOK-SASS-DIFF (full 6-shape)** — Per-shape hexa-emit vs nvcc CUDA C reference SASS instruction count comparison across all 6 cookbook WMMA kernels (extends commit `a1f9d80b`'s step1-only diff). nvcc 12.0.140 + cuobjdump on ubu-2 RTX 5070. Results: **step1_single_tile 80=80 (1.000 equal)** · **step2_multitile 320 vs 272 (1.176 hexa heavier +17.6%)** · **step3_multiwarp 336 vs 416 (0.808 hexa leaner −19.2%)** · **step4_cp_async 256 vs 928 (0.276 non-comparable — nvcc uses `cuda::pipeline` + `cooperative_groups::memcpy_async` state machine; hexa uses raw `cp.async.cg` + `wait_all`)** · **step5_tf32 144=144 (1.000 equal — was nvcc-generated)** · **composite_perf 352 vs 416 (0.846 hexa leaner −15.4%)**. Across 5 directly-comparable shapes: **hexa SASS 0.81-1.18× nvcc** (typical codegen variation). Stash 1's "hexa 53.9% of nvcc SASS" claim conclusively **REFUTED** across the full cookbook. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pE_cookbook_sass_diff_2026_05_21/` (6× `step<N>_ref.cu` + `.cubin` + `.ptx` + `result.json`)
- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SUBDIV-NUMERIC-EQ** 🛸 — vec-sub + vec-div MIR shapes silicon-validated on Apple M3 (cherry-pick `ca49aea1` from N2 sub-agent worktree, codegen now recognises **5 shapes**: vec-add + vec-mul + vec-sub + vec-div + vec-scale). `vec_sub` (3-buffer) **byte-eq** (max|Δ|=0, byte_mismatch=0/1024). `vec_div` **≤1 ULP** (max_ulp=1, 284/1024 cells deviate by ≤1 ULP) — Apple M3 GPU likely decomposes IEEE FP32 divide into `rcp + mul`, which is the standard GPU compromise (cuBLAS / Metal Performance Shaders both do this; not a codegen issue). Falsifier PASS criterion = byte-eq for arith with no decomposition + ≤4 ULP for divide. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_subdiv_2026_05_21/` (vec_sub.metal/.air/.metallib + vec_div.metal/.air/.metallib + host_subdiv.swift + result.json)
- [x] **F-RFC067-HGEMM-SCALEUP-HEXA (full 5-shape via shape-port)** — N4 sub-agent fired hand-emit PTX variants `wmma_{384,512,768,1024}x{...}_grid.ptx` produced by scaling the 256-shape's address-arithmetic constants + WMMA stride operands (microcode + 16-warp 4×4 block layout identical across all 5). Re-measured 5-shape ratios on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (200 timed launches per shape, 20 warmup, `cudaEventRecord` per-iter sync): **M=256 ratio 0.767** · **M=384 ratio 0.740** · **M=512 ratio 0.417** · **M=768 ratio 0.350** · **M=1024 ratio 0.287**. Hexa TFLOPS: 3.50 · 9.67 · 10.42 · 16.69 · 15.61. cuBLAS TFLOPS: 4.56 · 13.06 · 24.97 · 47.66 · 54.34. **Monotonic degradation** as M grows — naive K-loop is bandwidth-bound, lacks shared-memory tiling + software pipelining + async copies + split-K. Matches the optimiser-gap pattern documented in `reference_ptx_diff_perf_oracle` memory. M=256 ratio 0.767 matches commit `d9b737a2` (methodology stability across two fires). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pD_hgemm_followon_2026_05_21/` (host.c 440 lines + 4 new PTX + result.json). Honest scope: 4 new PTX are HAND-emit (not from compiler codegen); compiler `nvptx_target.hexa` still shape-locked at 256 — variable-M emission via the same compiler path is a follow-on (would benefit from RFC 071 P3 module-loader bridge to drive MIR → PTX from source); no numeric correctness check at new shapes (timing only — shape-port preserves WMMA microcode so correctness inherits from M=256)

Follow-up candidates: 4-warp 32×32 CTA (64×64 output, fewer warps, vectorised cp.async size=16) + `.maxnreg 32` to force spill over occupancy collapse + `ldmatrix`-based shared→fragment. - [x] **F-RFC071-NVPTX-SHFL-BFLY-B32 (N71-A, `9d21356c` + `7671d7db`)** 🛸 — `gpu_warp_shuffle_xor(v, lane_mask) -> u32` wired to NVPTX codegen. Emits `shfl.sync.bfly.b32 %r<dst>, %r<src>, %r<mask>, 0x1f, 0xffffffff;`. `bfly` mode XORs caller's lane id with mask operand → canonical primitive for warp-reduce butterfly (mask = 16, 8, 4, 2, 1 reduces 32 lanes pairwise). `0x1f` lane-mask+clamp-mode selector (full warp); `0xffffffff` membermask covering all 32 warp lanes (CUDA __FULL_MASK). Mirrors `gpu_warp_shuffle` shape — same U32 dst bank, same `%r<id>` register operands. **NEW const**: `PTX_OP_SHFL_SYNC_BFLY_B32`. **Classifier rule** added → NVPTX_RKIND_U32. Register count: 38/thread (vs N76 30 = +8 for NXT frags; well under 64 budget — NO occupancy collapse). **Mechanism FALSIFIED**: ptxas (CUDA 12.0) reordered SASS — PTX intent `ldmatrix NXT → ldmatrix NXT → mma CUR → mma CUR` but observed SASS at K-loop body shows `HMMA → LEA → HMMA → LDSM (after HMMA) → LDSM`. ptxas saw `rA,rB` written AFTER mma reads `ra,rb`, so all 4 instructions def-use-independent → chose alternate ordering minimizing live-range overlap. **Static PTX-level overlap invisible to scheduling control**. **3 explanations consistent with null**: (1) ptxas auto-pipelines cross-iteration regardless of static schedule (2) mma is NOT bottleneck at M≥768 (currently 23% of RTX 5070 134 TFLOPS HGEMM peak; cuBLAS at 50% = 2.16× gap too large for ldmatrix latency hiding alone) (3) RTX 5070 sm_120 may OoO-issue independent LDSM/HMMA pipes regardless of static ordering. **Remaining N76-list candidates**: single-buffered D output staging + K-loop unroll for ILP + larger output tile (64×64 → 128×128). - [x] **F-RFC067-HEXA-SGEMM-MMA-M16N8K32 (N90, ISA-LAYER FALSIFIED)** — **HARDWARE-ILLEGAL shape for FP16 multiplicands on all NVIDIA tensor-core generations through Blackwell sm_120**. ptxas rejects `mma.sync.aligned.m16n8k32.f32.f16.f16.f32` with `Illegal matrix shape '.m16n8k32' for instruction 'mma'` on **all 6 shapes / all arch targets (sm_90/90a/120/120a) / all ptxas versions (12.0.140, 12.9.86, driver-JIT 13000)**. Sanity cross-check with `m16n8k32.s32.s8.s8.s32` got DIFFERENT error (vector-size mismatch) → confirms ptxas accepts `.m16n8k32` shape token, but only for sub-byte int types. **Root cause (PTX ISA 8.7 §9.7.13.4.13)**: `m16n8k32` defined exclusively for sub-byte integer multiplicands (`.s8`/`.u8`/`.s4`/`.u4`/`.b1`). K-doubling comes from packing more sub-byte elements into same register footprint — **physically impossible for 2-byte FP16**. FP16 supported shapes only: `m8n8k4`, `m16n8k8`, `m16n8k16`. **Falsification more fundamental than target-bump** (task's honest-scope category): instruction simply doesn't exist for FP16 on any NVIDIA HW. **Peak TFLOPS N/A** (6/6 PTX load failures at driver-JIT, kernel never launched). cuBLAS re-measured 67.13 TFLOPS @ M=1536 (matches N77 baseline within variance). N77 36.06 / ratio 0.533 remains current `mma.sync`-path peak. **Path forward for "more arithmetic per mma issue on FP16"**: Hopper `wgmma.mma_async.sync.aligned` (sm_90+) or Blackwell `tcgen05.mma` (sm_100+) — different instruction classes (descriptor-based shared mem + async pipelining + different reg allocation). NOT a drop-in shape swap; multi-session refactor. Within `mma.sync` semantics, remaining levers: CTA output-tile (currently 64×64), pipeline depth (currently 2-slot DB), ldmatrix layout. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pT_hexa_sgemm_m16n8k32_2026_05_21/` (PTX pure-ASCII addressing math correct; only mma instruction itself ISA-illegal)

- [x] **🛸 F-RFC067-HEXA-SGEMM-STACK-6STAGE-4WARP (N121, PARETO TRADE)** — N105 6-stage + N107 4-warp 64×64 stacked. Bit-exact PASS all 6 shapes (max_abs=0). **Peak 50.455 TFLOPS @ M=1536, ratio 0.7596 (vs N107 51.65 / 0.777) = -2.32% PEAK REGRESSION**. **BUT**: **M=256 ratio 1.1611 (vs N107 1.053) = STRONGER cuBLAS-BEAT (+10.28% TFLOPS)** + **M=384 ratio 0.980 near-parity (vs N107 0.868) = +8.48%**. **Pareto trade vs N107, NOT strict improvement**. Mechanism: PZ's shmem 24576 B (vs PY 8192, PW 49152) cuts effective occupancy 8 CTAs/SM (PY reg-bound) → **4 CTAs/SM** (PZ shmem-bound). At M=1536 with 576 CTAs queued on 40 SMs, scheduler already had ample inter-CTA latency hiding — deeper per-CTA pipeline buys nothing while paying occupancy cost. **Why small-M wins**: at M=256 (16 CTAs) + M=384 (36 CTAs), grid under-subscribed on 40 SMs (≤1 CTA/SM running) — HBM round-trip latency between K-blocks is real bottleneck; 5-in-flight cp.async pipeline masks that latency where scheduler can't. **Useful conclusion**: 6-stage cp.async is **ONLY worth it at under-subscribed grids (M ≲ 400 on 40-SM sm_120)**. Follow-up: hybrid 3-stage instead of 6 to preserve small-M win without 3× shmem cost. Shmem: PY 8192 / PW 49152 / **PZ 24576 B**. Registers 64/thd unchanged. PY-w8 doubles warps 4→8 at fixed 64×64 tile and achieves *higher* thread-occupancy (100% vs 67%) yet performs marginally worse than N107 within noise. If axis (2) genuinely mattered, PY-w8 should sit between N107 (51.65) and N89 (37.07) — instead it sits indistinguishable from N107. **N107 analysis "warp-count drop 32→4 = 8× occupancy lift" was MISATTRIBUTION** that conflated CTA/SM occupancy with warp count; at 128×128 tile + 32 warps you get 1 CTA/SM not because of warp count itself but because **big tile forces it**. The genuine independent warp-count axis is inert because kernel is **throughput-limited at mma + cp.async pipeline**, NOT latency-limited. **3-axis decomposition revised**: axis (1) ~+13 TFLOPS (dominant) · axis (2) ~0 (refuted as independent) · axis (3) ~+1 TFLOPS small modifier. Per-CTA budget = 94×128 = 12032 regs → ~5 CTAs/SM (vs N107's 8 CTAs/SM) — **occupancy halved**. (2) **Full-CTA `bar.sync 0` serializes producer's slot reuse** with consumer's 16-mma chain. cuBLAS canonical avoids via **named barriers** (bar.arrive + named bar.sync with asymmetric arrival counts) — out of single-session reach without TMA/cp.async.bulk primitives. (3) **Compute warps halved (4→2), per-warp mma doubled (8→16)** — total CTA-wide mma issue rate identical to N107 (32 mma/K-step), but concentrated into 2 warps gives scheduler fewer compute warps to hide ldmatrix/mma stalls behind. **Useful negative**: confirms role-imbalanced workload hypothesis. **Warp spec needs named barriers + cp.async.bulk (TMA) to deliver** — primitives hand-emit doesn't reach. N79's lesson (ptxas reorders SASS for independent ops) holds: hand-emit ceiling = occupancy + named-bar, not spec idea itself. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pZspec_hexa_sgemm_warp_spec_2026_05_22/`

- [x] **🛸🛸🛸🛸🛸 F-RFC067-HEXA-TMA-SWIZZLE128 PASS (N204, 0.85 CEILING SHATTERED — peak 0.992 ratio)** — TMA descriptor with CU_TENSOR_MAP_SWIZZLE_128B + matched ldmatrix on ubu-1 RTX 5070 sm_120. **All 6 shapes bit-exact PASS** (maxabs=maxrel=0). **Per-shape (cuBLAS / hexa / ratio / vs N200-full)**: **M=512 23.43/23.24/0.992 (+33.7pp)** · M=1024 51.07/48.42/**0.948** (+21.0pp) · M=2048 66.25/63.25/**0.955** (+17.8pp) · M=4096 69.37/67.42/**0.972** (+17.2pp) · M=6144 70.17/68.21/**0.972** (+17.5pp) · **M=8192 70.18/68.61/0.978 (+15.9pp)**. **0.85 CEILING SHATTERED at every shape**. **g3-honest confound**: SWIZZLE_128B requires TMA box innermost ≥128B → forced widening K_TILE 16→64 (2048B→8192B/tile). The win combines (1) bank-conflict elimination via swizzle + (2) TMA setup amortization over 4× more mma K-steps per outer iter. Cleanly attributing requires intermediate SWIZZLE_NONE+wide-box measurement (follow-on). **Both effects real and unavoidable structurally**. **Derivation**: Empirical PTX probe on ubu-1 (programming guide gave algebra but not exact fp16-atom XOR mask). Loaded `(row<<8)|col` pattern via TMA with each swizzle mode, dumped smem to discover mapping. **SWIZZLE_128B formula**: `byte_offset = m*128 + (atom_k XOR (m & 7)) * 16 + (k_fp16 % 8) * 2`. Matches CUTLASS Sw<3,4,3> algebra. nvcc `cuda::ptx::ldmatrix` + `cuda::ptx::cp_async_bulk_tensor` hit template-overload errors in CUDA 12.9 `mbarrier_try_wait_parity.h` — empirical probe more reliable. **Resources**: 66 regs/thd, 16400 B shmem/CTA. **One bring-up issue**: v1 fill (cyclic K-only `i%4`/`i%3`) made all C[m,n] expected=396 at K=6144. Hexa returned 396 uniformly (CPU-verified correct); cuBLAS HGEMM returned 264/396/528 mix (split-K reduction artifact on fully-periodic fill). v2 row-perturbed fill broke equal-cell pattern; all bit-exact PASS. **Cumulative M=8192 ratio progression**: N38 0.263 → N130 0.30 → N149 0.847 → N200-full 0.819 → N203 0.8434 → N205 0.8381 → **N204 0.978 (= effective cuBLAS PARITY)**. cuBLAS catch-up UNLOCKED on consumer Blackwell via mma.sync + TMA + SWIZZLE_128B (NOT wgmma per N195). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_ptma_swizzle128_2026_05_22/`

### 1g — RFC 075 Metal P4 silicon-fire (2026-05-21) 🛸

- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-ROOFLINE-PROBE** 🛸 — Apple M3 GPU roofline probe via hand-emit `kernels.metal` with 5 kernels (1op / 4op / 16op / 64op / 256op chained per cell) × 4 shapes (N=64K/256K/1M/4M). 50 timed launches per (kernel, N). Crossover regime at N=4M: 1op = 34.91 GB/s + 2.91 GFLOPS (memory-bound) · 16op = **52.37 GB/s peak + 69.83 GFLOPS** (bandwidth saturation) · 64op = 48.73 GB/s + **259.87 GFLOPS peak** (compute-bound) · 256op = 11.11 GB/s + 236.98 GFLOPS (register pressure or thermal). Hand-emit kernels are NOT codegen-produced (probe is for Apple M3 characterisation, not codegen validation)

g3 caveats:
- Single vec-add kernel shape (the only shape `codegen_emit_metal_msl` recognises today); general `MFunc` → MSL emit is multi-session follow-on
- USER-LOCAL Mac fire path: this kernel cannot run on ubu-2 x86_64 / RTX 5070 (the Mac and the Nvidia GPU lanes are now bi-platform validated and remain orthogonal)
- N=1024 (small); larger N + multi-threadgroup + reductions are follow-on cycles
- No perf measurement — silicon-fire correctness only; Metal vs cuBLAS / Metal Performance Shaders perf comparison is a separate cycle

### 1h — F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH: fused attention moat (structural-formal + wall ruled-out) (2026-05-25)

The §10 moat case cuBLAS structurally CANNOT do: a single fused flash-attention kernel computing `softmax(Q K^T/√d) V` with online-softmax tiling (running max + running sum), **never materializing the N×N score matrix S to HBM**. Hand-emit pure-ASCII PTX (`archive/fires/fusion_attention_flash_2026_05_25/flash_attn.ptx`), fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (sm_120, driver 580) against a cuBLAS-using baseline (`cublasGemmStridedBatchedEx` QK^T → write S → standalone softmax kernel → `cublasGemmStridedBatchedEx` ·V). GPU uncontended at fire time (0% util, no compute procs → timed wall taken, not deferred). **Verdict: 🔵 structural-formal + 🔴 wall axis ruled-out (g3 closed-negative — both terminal, both publishable).**

- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH structural (clause a)** 🔵 — PROVEN closed-form. fused **1 launch** vs baseline **3**; S-matrix HBM round-trip fused **0 B** vs baseline **4·N²·4 B** (O(N²) eliminated). Total-HBM ratio `R(N,d) = (5Nd+4N²)/(4Nd) = 1.25 + N/d` → **9.25× @512, 17.25× @1024, 33.25× @2048, 65.25× @4096** (d=64). hexa-native compiled `ratio_check.hexa` reproduces R exactly (`4×R(2048,64)=133 ⇒ 33.25`) → **🔵 SUPPORTED-FORMAL**. $0 structural oracle (`structural_oracle.c`, deterministic, no GPU) is the PRIMARY finding. Verdict: `.verdicts/fusion-attention-flash/F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH.txt`
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH ptxas-clean** — `flash_attn.ptx` pure-ASCII; `ptxas -arch=sm_80` rc=0, `-arch=sm_90` rc=0; driver-JIT load on sm_120 (`cuModuleLoadDataEx`, `CU_JIT_TARGET_FROM_CUCONTEXT`) rc=0
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH-NUMERIC** — fused output vs **f64 CPU reference** rel-err ≤ 1e-2 PASS at N∈{512,1024,2048,4096} d=64 (max_rel ~1e-6, three orders under tol). Baseline matches identically (validates the layout)
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH wall (clause b) — 🔴 FALSIFIED (ruled-out axis)** — cudaEvent, 20 warmup + 200 timed, median ms. fused(1 launch) vs baseline(3 launch): **0.415 vs 0.282 @512 · 0.823 vs 0.559 @1024 · 1.640 vs 1.143 @2048 · 3.788 vs 2.492 @4096**. The cuBLAS baseline is **1.4–1.5× FASTER at every shape**. The fused kernel is a naive 1-thread-per-query scalar online-softmax; cuBLAS runs QK^T and ·V on Tensor Cores. **Closed-negative: structural fusion ALONE does not win wall vs cuBLAS** — the moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is necessary but NOT sufficient. The ≥30% wall additionally requires the fused inner GEMMs at Tensor-Core throughput (wmma m16n8k* tiling over Q/K/V blocks, S in shared memory). This deterministically scopes the next cycle.
- **§10 box "Whole-program-fusion ≥30%" stays `[ ]`** — structural-only; the wall was measured and NOT won (g3 honesty — structural-only / closed-negative leaves the box open with the finding noted). §5b "Attention scoring fusion" remains `[ ]` pending the Tensor-Core fused kernel.

g3 caveats:
- The wall negative is specific to the NAIVE scalar fused kernel — it does NOT falsify the moat thesis; it falsifies "fusion alone suffices" and pre-registers the Tensor-Core fused-attention kernel as the next falsifier
- d=64 single-head, FP32 throughout (the GEMMs are small enough that the O(N²) S round-trip the baseline pays is not large vs its TC GEMM speed); longer-context / multi-head / fp16 may shift the crossover and is a follow-on
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile changes (@F f2) — CPU codegen files MD5-identical pre/post (`self/runtime.c`, `compiler/codegen/{x86_64_linux,arm64_darwin}.hexa` unchanged); the fire is hand-emit PTX + .c hosts only

### 1h — Whole-program-fusion epilogue: GEMM + bias + GeLU structural finding (2026-05-25) 🛸

The classic fused-epilogue case cuBLAS cannot do: GEMM + bias-add + GeLU activation in one kernel. A single hexa-emit kernel computing `C = GeLU(A@B + bias)` fuses the GEMM, the bias-add, and the GeLU into one epilogue and writes the M×N result to HBM ONCE. This is a `$0`-oracle + ptxas-clean codegen round; the **timed silicon fire is DEFERRED to a serial follow-up** (ubu-2 is shared — parallel timed fires contend and poison wall numbers). Branch `gpu-fusion-epilogue` (from origin/main `49fcf884`). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_epilogue_gemm_bias_gelu_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-GEMM-BIAS-GELU (structural oracle, PRIMARY finding)** 🔵 — `$0` deterministic launch/byte count (`tool/fusion_epilogue_structural_oracle.hexa`, compiled hexa, run on ubu-1). At the LLaMA-7B FFN shape (M=4096 N=11008 K=4096; C tensor 180 355 072 B): **FUSED = 1 launch + 1× M×N HBM C-write** vs **BASELINE (cuBLAS-using stack: `cublasSgemm` → bias-add kernel → GeLU kernel) = 3 launches + 3× M×N HBM C-write**. **launch reduction 66.667 % AND HBM-write reduction 66.667 %** — both clear the ≥30 % whole-program-fusion gate by construction. Shape-independent (256³ cross-check identical, since the C-write traffic depends only on M×N). Verdict persisted `.verdicts/fusion-epilogue-gemm-bias-gelu/fusion_epilogue_structural.txt`
- [x] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-PTXAS-CLEAN** 🔵 — `ptxas -arch=sm_80 fused_gemm_bias_gelu.ptx` on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0): **RC=0, 23 registers, 0 spill, 4264-byte cubin**. PTX pure ASCII, md5 `1d7380556da101b7e37017b79eed6f01`. GeLU via tanh-approx (`ex2.approx.f32` base-2 exp + `rcp.approx.f32`), GEMM FP32 `fma.rn.f32`, bias-add + activation fused before the single `st.global.f32`
- **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-WALL (timed advantage, DEFERRED-to-serial-follow-up)** — fused 1-launch kernel wall vs the 3-launch cuBLAS-using baseline wall on ubu-2 RTX 5070. Host launchers authored (`tool/fusion_epilogue_fused_host.c` 1-launch driver-API + `tool/fusion_epilogue_cublas_baseline.c` 3-launch cuBLAS stack, both rel-err ≤1e-2 vs f64 CPU ref). DEFERRED — shared host; this round is `$0`-oracle + ptxas-clean only. **GPU.md §10 ≥30 % box stays `[ ]` until this timed wall lands** (the structural advantage is proven; the timed flip needs the wall)

g3 caveats:
- The structural oracle counts launches + HBM C-write bytes — a deterministic real measurement. It is NOT a timed wall; the timed perf advantage is the deferred follow-on
- The fused kernel is a one-thread-per-output naive GEMM (correctness + fusion-structure demonstration), not a WMMA-tiled perf kernel — the fusion *advantage* (1 vs 3 launches, 1× vs 3× HBM C-write) is independent of the inner GEMM tiling
- cuBLAS-LT *does* have a limited `GELU_BIAS` epilogue; the baseline models the canonical NN-stack path using plain `cublasSgemm`/`cublasGemmEx` (no fused epilogue), which is what flame/PyTorch-eager-class stacks emit
- No LLVM (@F f1), no C-transpile change (@F f2) — CPU codegen byte-identical pre/post (only doc + new artifact/tool files added)

### 1h — F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT — launch-overhead amortization $0 oracle (2026-05-25) 🛸

The §5f launch-overhead-amortization case made concrete + ptxas-clean. A single fused hexa-emitted kernel computes the **5-op elementwise chain `y = residual + scale * GeLU(a*x + b)`** (mul · add · gelu · mul-by-scale · add-residual) in ONE launch, with t1..t4 living in registers; a per-op baseline issues the SAME chain as **5 separate kernel launches**, each round-tripping the working tensor through HBM (eager-stack / per-op-library semantics). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT**: the fused single-launch kernel beats the 5-launch baseline by ≥30% wall in the launch-bound regime. This cycle is the **$0 structural/projection oracle + ptxas-clean**; the timed silicon wall is DEFERRED-to-serial (ubu-2 shared). Artifact: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT structural advantage PROVEN ($0 oracle, exit 0)** 🛸 — deterministic hexa-native oracle (`oracle.hexa`, built native, exit 0). **Launch count: fused 1 vs baseline 5 (5.0× fewer)**. **HBM traffic/elem: fused 2R+1W=3 vs baseline 6R+5W=11 (3.67× more for baseline)**. **Closed-form wall projection** from MEASURED per-launch overhead (§1g F-RFC067-PB-TIMING, warm Nth-launch L=1 µs; conservative effective BW=200 GB/s): `wall_fused = L + Rf·c·n`, `wall_baseline = 5L + Rb·c·n`. Launch-bound (n→0): `pct_faster → 1 − 1/5 = 80%`. Bandwidth-bound (n→∞): `pct_faster → 1 − Rf/Rb = 1 − 3/11 = 72.7%`. **The 30%-crossover `n* = 2.5L/(c·(Rf − 0.70·Rb))` has `(Rf − 0.70·Rb) = (3 − 7.7) = −4.7 < 0` ⇒ n\* NEGATIVE ⇒ no crossover ⇒ the ≥30% advantage is UNCONDITIONAL across all n**. Sample curve: n=64 → 79.98% · n=1024 → 79.69% · n=65536 → 74.6% · n=1M → 72.88%. **The falsifier is over-satisfied** — it predicted a launch-bound-only crossover, but the fused kernel wins on BOTH the launch axis (1<5) AND the HBM-traffic axis (3<11), so the ≥30% wall win never drops below 30%. Verdict verbatim: `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort/fusion_launch_amort.txt`.
- [x] **ptxas-clean — `ptxas -arch=sm_80 -v` on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0)** — both PTX modules assemble clean, 0 spill. **fused_chain.ptx rc=0** (11 regs, 392 B cmem[0], 0 spill). **baseline_chain.ptx rc=0** (5 entries k1_mul/k2_add/k3_gelu/k4_mul_scale/k5_add_resid = 10/10/11/10/12 regs, all 0 spill). Pure ASCII (driver-JIT ptxas rejects non-ASCII PTX comments). Log: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/ptxas_clean.log`. ptxas is not a timed run (no GPU contention).
- [x] **numeric correctness harness** — `host_fusion_launch.c` (cuLaunchKernel + cuEvent timing, `tool/r067_p4_host.c` pattern) compares the fused kernel to an f64 CPU reference of the identical chain (tanh-approx GeLU), tol 1e-2 abs (tanh.approx.f32 ~2⁻¹¹ rel bound). Numeric PASS confirmation is part of the DEFERRED timed fire.
- [x] **TIMED SILICON WALL — CONFIRMED 2026-05-25** 🛸🛸 — `host_fusion_launch.c` fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (GPU 0% util pre-fire, uncontended, 20 warmup + 200 timed median) across n∈{1024, 16384, 262144, 4194304, 16777216}: fused beats the 5-launch baseline **73.1–76.2% wall UNCONDITIONALLY** — n=1024 74.1%/3.86× · n=16384 73.1%/3.72× · n=262144 76.2%/4.20× · n=4194304 74.6%/3.93× · n=16.7M 73.5%/3.77×, all ≥30% gate PASS, numeric max|Δ|=1.1e-5 (abs) PASS. **The closed-form projection [72.7%,80%] is CONFIRMED BY MEASUREMENT** (🟢 SUPPORTED-NUMERICAL). **This FLIPS the §10 "≥30% whole-program fusion advantage" box to `[x]`** (domain @goal · §5f launch-overhead axis). Verdict verbatim: `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort-wall/F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT-WALL.txt`.

g3 caveats:
- The 80% / 72.7% figures are a closed-form PROJECTION from a measured per-launch constant (L=1 µs) + a model (memory-bound elementwise; per-op kernel = bandwidth-limited) — NOT a measured wall. The serial timed fire is the empirical confirmation.
- The HBM-traffic count (3 vs 11) is the structural ground truth; it is exact, not modeled. The launch-count (1 vs 5) is exact. The PROJECTION layer (translating those into a ≥30% wall) is what the timed fire validates.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched.

### 1i — F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA — Tensor-Core fused flash-attention codegen (round 2 of 3) (2026-05-25) 🛸

The Tensor-Core successor to the round-1 naive-scalar flash-attention kernel (§13 / `archive/fires/fusion_attention_flash_2026_05_25/`), which lost its wall **1.4–1.5× slower** than cuBLAS because its inner QK^T and ·V GEMMs were scalar `fma` loops. This round re-authors the fused `softmax(QK^T/√d)·V` kernel with **both inner GEMMs on Tensor Cores** via `wmma.mma.sync m16n16k16` (f16 mul, f32 acc), the **S tile resident in SHARED MEMORY (never to HBM)**, and online softmax (running max + sum) on the smem S tile. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL**: clause (a) ptxas-clean + 1 launch + 0 S-HBM + Tensor-Core inner GEMMs; clause (b) [ROUND 3] beats cuBLAS-batched-TC-GEMM+softmax by ≥30% wall. **THIS round = codegen + ptxas-clean (3 arches) + $0 structural oracle (clause a); the timed wall (clause b) is DEFERRED-to-round-3** (parent runs timed fires serially — uncontended GPU). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_wmma_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **clause (a) — WMMA fused kernel EMITS + ptxas-clean (3 arches)** 🛸 — hand-emit `flash_attn_wmma.ptx` (RFC 067 WMMA cookbook + `compiler/codegen/nvptx_target.hexa::_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` emit family). Pure ASCII (0 non-ascii bytes). **ptxas `-arch=sm_80` rc=0** (48 regs, 5824 B smem, 0 spill, 392 B cmem) · **ptxas `-arch=sm_90` rc=0** (48 regs, 5824 B smem, 0 spill) · **driver-JIT `sm_120` rc=0** on the live RTX 5070 (`cuModuleLoadDataEx` + `CU_JIT_TARGET_FROM_CUCONTEXT`, entry `flash_attn_wmma` resolved 48 regs / 5824 B static smem — a LOAD probe, NO kernel launch, NO timing). **Footprint fits the RTX 5070 envelope** (§1f caps): 48 regs ≪ 65536/block, 5824 B smem = 11.8% of the 49152 B/block cap; S tile (1024 B) + O tile (4096 B) resident in smem.
- [x] **clause (a) — structural moat PRESERVED + Tensor-Core inner GEMMs confirmed** 🛸 — `$0` compiled-hexa oracle (`structural_oracle.hexa`, `hexa build` + run — `hexa verify` g5 is broken on both ubu hosts, so compiled-hexa per the round protocol; stdout verbatim in verdict): **1 launch vs baseline 3**, **0 S-HBM vs baseline 4·N²·4 B** (67 108 864 B @ N=2048), total-HBM ratio `R(N,d)=1.25+N/d` reproduced (4×R(2048,64)=133). **Static PTX ground-truth grep**: `wmma.mma.sync` **×5 distinct** (1× `mma.row.col` QK^T + 4× `mma.row.row` P·V over d=64) **vs round-1 ZERO** — the round-1 wall-loss root cause (scalar inner GEMMs) is ADDRESSED. **`st.global` ×1** — the ONLY HBM write is the final O; the S tile uses `wmma.store.d …shared.f32` exclusively ⇒ **S never touches HBM**.
- [x] **clause (b) ROUND-3 harness READY (NOT run)** — `fa_wmma_host.c` (fused launcher: IEEE f16 in/out, f64 CPU reference on the f16-rounded inputs, rel-err ≤ 1e-2, `cuEvent` 20 warmup + 200 timed median) + `fa_cublas_tc_baseline.c` (cuBLAS `CUBLAS_GEMM_DEFAULT_TENSOR_OP` 3-launch QK^T → softmax kernel → P·V, `cuEvent` timed). Both **`nvcc -c` compile-clean on ubu-2** (rc=0). Round-3 plan: serial uncontended fire at N∈{512,1024,2048,4096} d=64; win = `baseline_ms/fused_ms ≥ 1.30`.

g3 caveats:
- **WALL clause (b) — ROUND-3 FIRED 2026-05-25: 🔴 FALSIFIED.** Timed on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (uncontended, GPU 0% pre-fire, 20 warmup + 200 timed median, d=64): the fused single-CTA wmma kernel is **9.4–15.5× SLOWER** than the cuBLAS-TC 3-launch baseline — N=512 0.157 vs 0.0166 ms (9.4×) · N=1024 0.335 vs 0.0309 ms (10.8×) · N=2048 0.819 vs 0.0617 ms (13.3×) · N=4096 2.930 vs 0.189 ms (15.5×) — **AND numeric FAILs** (max_rel 2.6–4.8 > 1e-2 tol; max_abs ~3–6e-5). **Ruled-out axis (the round-3 finding):** Tensor-Core *instructions* alone do NOT win the wall. The round-2 kernel is **single-CTA** (S/P/O tiles + 48 regs resident in one block's smem) so it occupies **~1 of the RTX 5070's 48 SMs** while cuBLAS launches a grid of thousands of CTAs — the structural moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is real but dominated by a 47/48-SMs-idle parallelism deficit. Beating cuBLAS attention requires cuBLAS-grade **multi-CTA work distribution + occupancy + tiling** (flash-attention's actual design: one CTA per (query-block, head)), not just `wmma.mma.sync`. The clause-(a) verdict (🔵 codegen/structural) stands; clause (b) is a closed-negative. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-wmma-wall/F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL.txt`.
- **§10 box is NOT touched.** The "≥30% whole-program fusion" box is already `[x]` (flipped via the §5f launch-amortization axis, PR #1028). This GEMM-fusion (attention) axis needs its OWN round-3 timed Tensor-Core wall to win — flipping nothing here.
- The kernel keeps the S tile in shared memory and applies online softmax via a shared-mem round-trip of the S/O tiles (correct-by-construction, sidesteps the mma fragment lane→(row,col) layout) — a perf-relevant choice the round-3 fire measures; an in-fragment softmax is a follow-on optimization if the wall is close.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX); CPU codegen MD5 preserved (`x86_64_linux.hexa b50a2a3c…`, `arm64_darwin.hexa b0a397dc…`).

### 1j — F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA — multi-CTA wide-KV fused flash-attention (round 4) (2026-05-25) 🟠

The round-4 attack on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis after round-3's 🔴 wall loss. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA-WALL**: author a **CORRECT, multi-CTA** fused flash-attention kernel that saturates the SMs (keeping online softmax + S-in-shared-never-HBM + wmma inner GEMMs), then re-time vs cuBLAS-TC 3-launch — win = ≥30% faster (ratio ≤ 0.70). **Result: 🟠 QUANTIFIED-PARTIAL** — a correct multi-CTA kernel that closes the gap ~3–8× but does **not** beat cuBLAS-TC. Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_multicta_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **NUMERIC — round-3 "FAIL" was a METRIC ARTIFACT, kernel is CORRECT** 🟢 — round 3's reported `max_rel 2.6–4.8 = FAIL` came from the naive `|err|/(|want|+1e-6)` metric exploding on the **many near-zero attention output elements** (|want| ≪ 1e-6) — NOT a kernel bug. Under the honest **per-row-scaled + RMS** relative metric the round-3 *algorithm* is already correct, proven independently in clean CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` (rel_rowscale 5e-4, rms 2.6e-4, PASS). The shipped hand-PTX multi-CTA kernel `flash_attn_wmma_mcta` then PASSes numeric at all 4 shapes vs the f64 CPU ref: rel_rowscale **6.3e-4 / 5.6e-4 / 6.3e-4 / 7.1e-4** (N=512/1024/2048/4096), rms ~2.7e-4 — matching the CUDA-C oracle exactly (⇒ the hand-PTX WMMA fragment handling is correct).
- [x] **round-3 was ALSO already multi-CTA** — the round-3 grid was `N/16` CTAs (not single-CTA); the real deficit was **1 warp/CTA doing per-16-key serial online-softmax overhead**. The round-4 lever is **widening the KV tile from BK=16 to BK=256** (16 wmma key-subtiles per softmax round), amortizing the softmax+rescale overhead 16×.
- [x] **ptxas-clean (3 arches) + footprint** — pure ASCII (0 non-ascii bytes). **sm_80 rc=0** (41 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill, 392 B cmem) · **sm_90 rc=0** (32 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill) · **driver-JIT sm_120** loads + runs OK. 28864 B smem/CTA = **58.7% of the 49152 B/block cap (FITS)**; S(16×256)+O(16×64) resident in smem, never to HBM. **Grid occupancy:** `N/16` ⇒ **32 / 64 / 128 / 256 CTAs** (vs 48 SMs) — max grid saturation (multi-warp-per-CTA was MEASURED slower: cuts grid count + raises smem/CTA).
- [x] **TIMED WALL (clause b) — 🟠 PARTIAL** — ubu-2 RTX 5070 (clean, 0% util, 0 compute procs, cuEvent 20 warmup + 200 timed median, d=64). Shipped **hand-PTX fused vs cuBLAS-TC**: N=512 0.0566 vs 0.0167 ms (**3.40×**) · N=1024 0.114 vs 0.0308 ms (**3.70×**) · N=2048 0.244 vs 0.0617 ms (**3.96×**) · N=4096 0.954 vs 0.190 ms (**5.01×**). **Gap closure: round-3 9.4–15.5× → round-4 3.4–5.0×.** The CUDA-C-validated geometry floor (nvcc-vectorized scalar loops) is even tighter: **1.32 / 1.44 / 1.65 / 2.04×** — the hand-PTX scalar softmax/rescale loops are un-vectorized (~2–2.5× slower than nvcc's `ld.shared.v4`/unroll), so a hexa-codegen path with vectorized smem loads could approach this floor.

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Fused is still **1.3–5.0× slower** than cuBLAS-TC (ratio > 0.70) — the ≥30% GEMM-fusion-axis win is **not achieved**. Honest tier = 🟠.
- **Binding constraint identified:** at d=64 the **per-16×16-tile online-softmax overhead — NOT S-HBM traffic — is the wall**. cuBLAS amortizes its GEMMs over huge tiles the tiny 16×16 WMMA fused path cannot match; wide-KV amortization narrows but does not close this. The structural moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is real and preserved but not the bottleneck at this shape.
- **§10 box is NOT touched** — stays `[x]` only via the launch-amort axis (PR #1028). The GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper** — `paper_gate` forbids 🟠 partial sections; this is neither a ≥30% win nor a clean closed-negative (the kernel works, it just loses the wall).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX); the CUDA-C `.cu` files are correctness/geometry oracles only, not the shipped fused path. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1k — F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP — full dimensional-decomposition sweep · KV-split hypothesis (round 5) (2026-05-25) 🟠→closed-neg

The round-5 attack: map the **complete parallel-decomposition space** of the fused `softmax(QK^T/√d)·V` kernel vs cuBLAS-TC 3-launch, and specifically test whether the **KV-SPLIT (z-axis, flash-decoding)** dimension closes the small-N occupancy gap left by round-4 (N=512 grid = only 32 CTAs < 48 SMs). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP-WALL**. Swept **153 configs** = N{512,1024,2048,4096} × Bq{16,32,64} × kv_split{1,2,4,8,16} × BK{64,128,256}, d=64 — **all numeric PASS** (rel_rowscale ≤ 1e-2 vs f64 CPU ref). Tool: a CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` **flash-decoding oracle** (2-kernel: partial-O + LSE-merge), authored correctly — `kv_split=1` reduces EXACTLY to the round-4 algorithm (max_abs 4.02796e-05 identical). **Result: 🟠 QUANTIFIED-PARTIAL → closed-negative.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_decomp_2026_05_25/`; ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-attn-decomp-2026-05-25/`.

- [x] **KV-SPLIT CLOSES the small-N occupancy gap — user hypothesis CONFIRMED** 🟢 — N=512 Bq16: occupancy **32 → 128 CTAs** (kv=1→kv=4), wall **0.146 → 0.058 ms** = **2.53× intra-framework speedup**, reaching **parity with the round-4 single-kernel** (0.0568 ms) despite the 2-pass partial-O+merge tax. The benefit **saturates** at the split K where ctas_partial ≥ ~48 SMs (N=512 plateaus at kv=4=128 CTAs; **kv=8/16 REGRESS** via over-subscription + merge cost).
- [x] **KV-split is a SMALL-N-ONLY lever** — at N≥2048 the grid is already saturated by `N/Bq` alone, so KV-split adds only the partial-O HBM round-trip tax (grows O(N·split·d)): decomp-best **0.668 ms vs round-4 single-kernel 0.245 ms @ N=2048 (2.7× WORSE)**. Net-neutral at small N, net-negative at large N.
- [x] **BK=256 confirmed best** within every fixed (N,Bq,kv) (round-4 finding re-confirmed); **Bq>16 uniformly slower** (cuts grid, the opposite of what small-N needs).
- [x] **OPTIMUM PER SHAPE (vs cuBLAS-TC)** — N=512 Bq16/kv4/BK128 **3.47×** · N=1024 Bq32/kv4/BK256 **5.88×** · N=2048 Bq64/kv4/BK256 **10.82×** · N=4096 Bq16/kv8/BK256 **13.17×**. Best overall = **3.47× @ N=512**.

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Best ratio 3.47× (> 0.70). The ≥30% GEMM-fusion-axis win is **not achieved** by any decomposition. Honest tier = 🟠.
- **Closed-negative on the decomposition axis:** *no dimensional decomposition of hand-PTX flash-attn beats cuBLAS-TC at d=64.* KV-split trades **occupancy ↔ HBM-traffic** — it does not breach the round-4 binding constraint (per-16×16-tile online-softmax overhead vs cuBLAS huge-tile GEMM efficiency). The GEMM-tile-efficiency wall is **confirmed fundamental**.
- The 2-pass oracle's absolute walls carry a partial-O HBM round-trip + 2nd-launch tax the round-4 single-kernel avoids; the **decomposition trend** is isolated within the consistent 2-pass frame, with the round-4 single-kernel given as the absolute cross-reference.
- **§10 box is NOT touched** — stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper.** Captured as a closed-negative finding in the discovery log + ledger; `paper_gate` not triggered (no ≥30% win; the closed-negative is a re-confirmation of the round-4 wall via a new axis, not a fresh disproof worth a paper scaffold).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX path); the CUDA-C `.cu` is a correctness/decomposition oracle only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1m — F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE — N204 roofline-GEMM-toolkit transplant (round 7) (2026-05-25) 🟠→closed-neg

The round-7 attack: hexa ALREADY hits the GEMM roofline standalone (N204 "TMA SWIZZLE_128B" reached **cuBLAS 0.978 parity @ M=8192**, PRs #333/#335) — the round-4/5 fused attention lost its wall (best 3.47×) NOT because hexa can't do roofline GEMM, but because the fused kernel's inner QK^T and P·V GEMMs were naive (single-warp, 16×16 wmma tiles, no TMA, no double-buffer, no swizzle). This round transplants the proven N204 roofline toolkit (TMA `cp.async.bulk.tensor` + double-buffered K/V tiles + 64×64 large `mma.sync.m16n8k16` tiles + 4-warp 2×2 layout) into the fused `softmax(QK^T/√d)·V` inner GEMMs and measures % of the cuBLAS-TC + theoretical roofline. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE**: ratio ≤ 1.10 vs cuBLAS-TC on at least one shape (N∈{2048,4096}, d=64) AND report achieved % of the sm_120 FP16 tensor-core roofline. **Result: 🟠 INSUFFICIENT (target NOT hit) + closed-negative finding.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_roofline_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **clause (a) — kernel emits + ptxas-clean** 🛸 — hand-emit `flash_attn_tma_v2_{2048,4096}.ptx` (pure ASCII, 0 non-ascii bytes). **ptxas `-arch=sm_120a` rc=0** (68 regs, 0 spills, 1 barrier, 8 B stack). 5 `cp.async.bulk.tensor` (TMA) + 64 `mma.sync.aligned.m16n8k16` + 32 `ldmatrix` + 1 `st.global` (final O only — S NEVER to HBM, moat preserved). cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor = **1 CTA/SM** (smem 99136 B vs optin/SM 102400 B).
- [x] **clause (b) — NUMERIC PASS via fa_mma_oracle.cu + silicon fire** 🟢 — both shapes pass the honest per-row-scaled metric: N=2048 rel_rowscale 6.11e-4 / rms_rel 2.72e-4 · N=4096 rel_rowscale 7.14e-4 / rms_rel 2.72e-4. Matches the round-4 oracle EXACTLY (max_abs 3.11e-5 @ N=4096 identical) → algorithmic equivalence confirmed.
- [x] **🛸 MMA-FRAGMENT-MAP DISCOVERY** 🟢 — the round-7 probe campaign (`probe2.cu` + `probe3.cu`) empirically established that **`mma.sync.m16n8k16 .trans` + `ldmatrix.x4` performs an 8×8-BLOCK transpose within each 16×16 fragment, NOT a full 16×16 transpose**. Non-trans + `mma.row.col` gives `C = A·B^T` (err 1e-7 MATCH). The P·V GEMM (contraction along V rows) therefore CANNOT use the same `.trans`-B path as QK^T; **v2 pre-transposes V into a separate smem buffer** so the proven non-trans path drives both GEMMs (probe3 err 6e-8 MATCH). Non-obvious empirical fact about m16n8k16 ldmatrix.x4 semantics not surfaced by PTX ISA narrative reading.
- [x] **🔴 clause (c) — TIMED WALL ratio NOT ≤1.10** — fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120, GPU 0% util, 0 compute procs (uncontended). 20 warmup + 200 timed cuEvent median:
  - **N=2048**: fused **0.324864 ms** / cuBLAS-TC **0.061568 ms** → **ratio 5.276× SLOWER**. Fused 3.31 TFLOPS · cuBLAS 17.44 TFLOPS.
  - **N=4096**: fused **1.281312 ms** / cuBLAS-TC **0.186624 ms** → **ratio 6.866× SLOWER**. Fused 3.35 TFLOPS · cuBLAS 23.01 TFLOPS.
- [x] **% OF ROOFLINE** (stated assumptions: sm_120 RTX 5070 from §1f caps — 48 SM · 2.542 GHz · 192-bit bus):
  - **% of cuBLAS HGEMM achievable ceiling (~70.2 TFLOPS @ N204 M=8192)**: N=2048 **4.71%** · N=4096 **4.77%**.
  - **% of theoretical FP16-TC peak (48 SM × 4 TC × 256 FMA × 2 FLOP × 2.542 GHz = 249.9 TFLOPS)**: N=2048 **1.32%** · N=4096 **1.34%**.
  - cuBLAS-TC 3-launch attention reaches 17.4 / 23.0 TFLOPS = 24.8% / 32.8% of its own HGEMM ceiling — so cuBLAS's attention itself is ~3-4× off roofline.
- [x] **GAP-CLOSURE TRAJECTORY (final)** — round-3 9.4-15.5× → round-4 3.4-5.0× → round-5 3.47× → **ROUND-7 5.3-6.9× (REGRESSION)**.
- [x] **OCCUPANCY ATTRIBUTION (direct measurement)** — `cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor` on the real fn returned **1 CTA/SM** (smem-bound). At N=2048 grid=32 CTAs → **only 32 of 48 SMs populated (66.7% SM coverage)**. At N=4096 grid=64 → 48 SMs 1-CTA + 16 CTAs queued for serialized second wave. Round-4's BM=16 kernel had **8 CTAs/SM**; the 64×64 attention tile multiplies the resident-set smem 8× (Q + K[2] + V[2] + V^T[2] + S + P + O all simultaneously) → occupancy collapse.
- [x] **DOUBLE-BUFFER ATTRIBUTION (paired-shape A/B)** — single-buffer occupancy-test variant (`flash_attn_tma_sb`, smem 74560 B, same 1 CTA/SM): wall 0.324896 ms. v2 double-buffer: 0.324864 ms. **Δ 0.01% — double-buffer ZERO BENEFIT here**: kernel is occupancy-bound, not DMA-bound; the TMA overlap opportunity is unrealized (no parallel compute to hide loads behind at 1 CTA/SM, only 4 warps with mma chain that can't overlap its own smem dependencies on the same slot).

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Best ratio 5.27× (> 1.10 by 4.8×). Pre-registered target NOT hit. Honest tier = 🟠 INSUFFICIENT + closed-negative finding on the technique axis.
- **CLOSED-NEGATIVE (terminal):** *the N204 standalone-GEMM roofline toolkit DOES NOT TRANSPLANT to fused flash-attention.* The 64×64 tile that buys roofline-GEMM performance for a standalone GEMM COSTS attention occupancy because fused attention has fundamentally different smem residency (Q + K + V + V^T + S + P + O simultaneously resident — multiple O(BM × BK) and O(BM × d) tiles). The technique is correct in isolation (numeric PASS, ptxas-clean) but the architectural fit is wrong for this kernel. **Which N204 technique helped most: NONE moved the wall positively.** Rank by attribution: 64×64 tile (BACKFIRED, the main regressor) > TMA loads (NEUTRAL, save HBM but no occupancy to absorb) > double-buffer (ZERO) > swizzle (NOT APPLIED in v2 because the .trans-B path is invalid for P·V).
- **§10 box is NOT touched** — stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper.** ORANGE INSUFFICIENT + re-confirmation of an already-CLOSED-NEGATIVE wall via a new failed-axis — `paper_gate` forbids per project.tape `paper_significance`.
- **Next-round wedge (recommendation):** shallower tile BM=32 (or BM=16 with multi-warp) + REGISTER-RESIDENT O (acc in registers, not smem) + selective TMA to restore ≥2-4 CTAs/SM occupancy WITHOUT abandoning TMA loads. Smem budget then ~34-50 KB → 2 CTAs/SM, doubling occupancy.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX path); `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1n — F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTIWARP — multi-warp BM=64 + cp.async K/V double-buffer (round 10, campaign capstone attempt) (2026-05-26) 🟠

The round-10 attack on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A, taking R9's (#1121) next-wedge prescription literally. R9 diagnosed the d=64 16×16 **single-warp** tile as **latency/dependency-bound** (occupancy was plenty at 24-28 CTAs/SM): the per-tile row-reduction between the QK^T mma and the P·V mma sits on the critical path with no other warp's work to hide it. R10 breaks that floor two ways on the R9 reg-S + smem-scratch-reduce base (NOT warp-shuffle — R9 closed-negatived that): **(1) multi-warp BM=64** — 4 warps/CTA (block=128), each owning 16 *independent* query rows (warp w → rows [w·16..w·16+15], no cross-warp softmax), the 4 warps **sharing one K/V smem tile** (loaded once per CTA → no HBM-traffic multiplication); **(2) cp.async.cg K/V double-buffer** — the next K/V tile prefetches async while the current tile computes, overlapping HBM load latency with the mma pipeline. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTIWARP**: numeric PASS + ptxas-clean + beats cuBLAS-stack (`fused_ms < cublas_stack_ms`) on ≥1 (N,d) shape, d=64. **Result: 🟠 INSUFFICIENT (best-of-campaign, does NOT cross 1.0×).** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attn_multiwarp_2026_05_26/`.
- [x] **NUMERIC — all 4 shapes PASS** 🟢 — `fa_mw_cpasync` vs f64 CPU ref + NaN/Inf hard-fail counter: rel_rowscale **5.41e-4 / 5.67e-4 / 6.11e-4 / 7.14e-4** (N=512/1024/2048/4096), naninf=**0**, bit-equivalent in tolerance to R8/R9. ptxas-clean 0-spill sm_80 (91 reg) / sm_90a (93 reg) / sm_90 (93 reg); **14336 B smem ≪ 49152 B cap** (double-buffer K/V 8192 B + per-warp scratch). Occupancy reg-bound at **5 CTAs/SM × 4 warps = 20 warps/SM** (vs R9 25 warps/SM single-warp → occupancy still NOT binding).
- **WALL — 🔴 FALSIFIED as a WIN / 🟠 best-of-campaign gap-closure.** cuEvent 20 warmup + 200 timed median, ubu-2 RTX 5070 (0% util pre-fire, ~0.4% repro): ratio vs cuBLAS-stack **1.613× / 1.309× / 1.186× / 1.149×** @ N=512/1024/2048/4096 — best **1.149× @ N=4096** (14.9% BELOW cuBLAS). Does NOT cross 1.0× on any shape → the pre-registered win condition is NOT met. **Gap-closure: R9 best 1.662× (same session) → R10 1.149×;** R10 is **1.447× FASTER than R9 single-warp** at N=4096 (0.2173 vs 0.3145 ms) — the fastest fused attention of the whole campaign.
- **LEVER ISOLATION (controlled A/B — `fa_mw_noasync` drops only cp.async, single-buffer synchronous load):** **cp.async double-buffer is the DOMINANT lever** — mw+cpasync is **1.34× / 1.46× / 1.50× / 1.40×** faster than no-async multi-warp. The **multi-warp lever alone** (no-async vs R9) is **1.12× / 1.28× / 1.37× / 1.04×** — real but smaller, and **fades to 1.04× at N=4096**. BOTH levers moved it; overlapping the HBM K/V load with the mma pipeline closed most of the gap.
- **RESIDUAL BOTTLENECK:** still latency-bound, but the exposed latency moved from R9's per-tile row-reduction to (1) the intra-warp QK^T-mma → row-reduce → P·V-mma dependency chain each warp still serializes, and (2) the per-K-tile `__syncthreads` barrier across the 4 warps sharing the double-buffered smem. At d=64 the wmma tile is only 4 d-tiles deep → arithmetic intensity too low to saturate the tensor cores vs cuBLAS's two big TC GEMMs; grid=N/64 also under-fills the 48 SMs at N≤2048. NOT bandwidth, NOT occupancy.
- **§10 box is NOT touched** — stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A remains NOT-won at d=64 (no 1.0× cross). No new closure row flipped.
- **No paper.** 🟠 INSUFFICIENT — `paper_gate` / `paper_significance` (project.tape) forbid a paper without a terminal WIN; paper triggers only on a GREEN 1.0×-cross capstone.
- **Next-round wedge (recommendation):** (a) **2-stage software COMPUTE pipeline** — overlap the P·V mma of K-tile j with the QK^T mma of tile j+1 to break the intra-warp 3-phase chain that is now the floor (cp.async already overlaps the LOAD; this overlaps the COMPUTE phases); (b) **head dim d≥128 sweep** — cuBLAS's S=N×N HBM round-trip cost is fixed but fused TC utilization rises with deeper d-tiles, so the fused path may favor larger d where R10's 4-d-tile arithmetic-intensity ceiling lifts; (c) **wgmma** (sm_90 async warpgroup mma) for higher per-instruction TC throughput. Do NOT retry warp-shuffle softmax (R9 closed-negative) nor expect multi-warp-alone to help at large N (R10 measured it fades to 1.04×).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX / CUDA-oracle path); `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1o — F-FUSION-ATTN-DSWEEP-PIPE — head_dim sweep + 2-stage compute pipeline (round 11) (2026-05-26) 🟠→near-ceiling-closed-neg

The round-11 attack taking R10's (#1135) two next-wedges literally — two coupled probes on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A. **(A) head_dim sweep:** parameterize R10's multi-warp BM=64 + cp.async kernel over head_dim `D` (`DTILES = D/16` d-tiles), fire at d∈{64,128,256} × N∈{1024,2048,4096}. Hypothesis: at d≥128 the fused inner-GEMM arithmetic intensity rises → the fused path may CROSS ≤1.0× (above cuBLAS-stack). **(B) 2-stage COMPUTE pipeline** at best-d: overlap the P·V mma of K-tile j with the QK^T mma of tile j+1 (break the intra-warp dependency chain R10 found is now the floor — distinct from cp.async which overlapped the LOAD). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-DSWEEP-PIPE**: WIN = `fused_ms < cublas_stack_ms` (ratio ≤1.0×) on ≥1 (N,d). **Result: 🟠 NEAR-CEILING CLOSED-NEGATIVE — BOTH levers FALSIFIED; the d-lever moves the WRONG way.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attn_dsweep_pipe_2026_05_26/`.
- **BASELINE INTEGRITY (instrument-first, g3):** the fused kernel is FP16-Tensor-Core; the fair baseline is the FP16 cuBLAS-TC 3-launch stack. A launch-decomposition probe (`cublas_probe.cu`) caught that a NAIVE one-thread-per-row softmax was a **13× SLOWER STRAWMAN** (softmax kernel alone 2.154 ms @ N=4096 d=64 vs the two GEMMs' 0.316 ms) — a 🟢 against it would have been **DISHONEST and was REJECTED.** Fixed to an OPTIMIZED block-per-row parallel-reduction softmax; corrected cuBLAS-TC = **0.176 ms @ N=4096 d=64**, matching R10's recorded 0.189 ms baseline. All ratios below use the fair baseline.
- [x] **NUMERIC — all 12 measured shapes PASS** 🟢 — `fa_dsweep` per-row-scaled rel **5.6–7.1e-4**, naninf=0 at all 9 (N,d); d=64 rows bit-identical to R10 (faithful parameterization). `fa_pipe` (probe B, d=64) PASS bit-identical to R10. ptxas-clean 0-spill: `fa_dsweep` sm_80 **91 / 148 / 247 reg**, smem **14336 / 22528 / 38912 B** @ d=64/128/256 (all ≪ 49152 B cap); `fa_pipe` 104 reg / 18432 B.
- **PROBE (A) WALL — 🔴 d-lever FALSIFIED IN THE WRONG DIRECTION.** ratio fused/cuBLAS-TC WORSENS monotonically with d: d=64 **{1.229, 1.225, 1.234}** · d=128 **{2.149, 1.673, 1.752}** · d=256 **{2.967, 2.290, 2.217}** @ N={1024,2048,4096}. Best ratio **1.225× @ d=64 N=2048** never crosses ≤1.0×. **Root cause:** cuBLAS's two big TC GEMMs are dominated by the d-INDEPENDENT N×N S HBM round-trip (cuBLAS @ N=4096 barely slows: 0.176 → 0.233 → 0.354 ms); the fused per-warp **serial d-tile loop** (`DTILES` mma + scale_o + P-repack on the critical chain) scales LINEARLY with d (0.217 → 0.409 → 0.786 ms). Raising head_dim **WIDENS** the gap — the d-trend DIVERGES from a crossover. d-lever RULED OUT.
- **PROBE (B) WALL — 🔴 compute-pipeline FALSIFIED.** At best-d=64: v1 (hoist QK^T but serialize the load) = **+18.9..27.9% SLOWER** (confirms R10's cp.async LOAD-overlap is dominant — do not trade it away). v2 (race-free **triple-buffer** K+V keeping 2-deep load overlap AND hoisting QK^T(j+1) from the prefetched slot, numeric bit-identical) = **+4.9 / +4.2 / +2.4% SLOWER** than R10 @ N=1024/2048/4096. The intra-warp QK^T→reduce→P·V chain is **NOT an exposed pipeline bubble** — with 4 warps × 20 warps/SM the scheduler already interleaves the independent wmma streams; the hoist's extra `__syncthreads` + register pressure (93→104) cost more than any gain. Campaign-best ratio stays R10's **1.149× @ N=4096 d=64**.
- **§10 box is NOT touched** — stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A remains NOT-won at d∈{64..256} (no 1.0× cross). The two most-plausible remaining levers (deeper d, compute-overlap) are now both RULED OUT — the inner-GEMM TC-utilization gap is FUNDAMENTAL at these shapes. A valid g3 near-ceiling closed-negative.
- **No paper.** 🟠 — `paper_gate` / `paper_significance` (project.tape) forbid a paper without a terminal WIN; the closed-negative rules out two axes but is not a ≤1.0× capstone.
- **Next untried lever:** (a) **wgmma** (sm_90 async warpgroup mma m64nNk16) — the ONE lever not yet tried that directly attacks the TC-utilization gap (bigger per-instruction tile → higher arithmetic intensity per issue); (b) **FP8 e4m3** on Blackwell TCs to double throughput; (c) accept fused attention at d∈{64..256} as a measured near-ceiling and pivot the fusable-axis @goal to an op-pair where cuBLAS truly forces an HBM round-trip AND the fused inner GEMM can saturate TCs. Do NOT re-sweep d (ruled out) nor re-pipeline the compute at d=64 (ruled out).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED; `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.
